  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ec4d6abb-0ffa-4d23-bf09-e7c4284392c7'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText15425588694333210762" style="display:none">"Love in my world usually ended up with someone hearing 'I smite thee!' as she was cursed to be some lame flower for the rest of her life." <br /><br />For three years, Alexandria has lived among mortals—pretending to be like them and trying to forget the duty she'd been trained to fulfill as a child of a mortal and a demigod. At seventeen, she's pretty much accepted that she's a freak by mortal standards… and that she'll never be prepared for that duty. <br /><br />According to her mother, that’s a good thing. <br /><br />But as every descendant of the gods knows, Fate has a way of rearing her ugly head. A horrifying attack forces Alex to flee Miami and try to find her way back to the very place her mother had warned her she should never return—the Covenant. Every step that brings her closer to safety is one more step toward death… because she's being hunted by the very creatures she'd once trained to kill. <br /><br />The daimons have found her.</span>

<div id="review_181644391" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/181644391" />
    <a title="Arlene" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene"><img alt="Arlene" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347048609p2/1746727.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/181644391?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arlene" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arlene" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene">Arlene</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Vampire Academy</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Arlene by: </span>
      Street Corner Bookers - Alexa &amp; Crystal
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=read-2011">read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=greek-mythology">greek-mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=ya-paranormal">ya-paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer181644391" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15394240210121805778"><i>Swinging with all my might, I slammed the bottom of the lamp into the daimon’s head. The sickening thud it made pleased me in a way that would’ve concerned guidance counselors across the nation.</i><br/><br/><b>Addicting!!</b><br/><br/>I picked up the <b>Daimon</b> prequel in anticipation for the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9680718.Half_Blood__Covenant___1_' title='Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout' rel='nofollow noopener'>Half-Blood</a> ARC I’ll be reviewing soon and WOW! What a great kickoff to a series I know is going to have me on the edge of my seat. Definitely a storyline I can fall into with a great cast and a perfectly crafted paranormal element.<br/><br/>The writi</span>
  <span id="freeText15394240210121805778" style="display:none"><i>Swinging with all my might, I slammed the bottom of the lamp into the daimon’s head. The sickening thud it made pleased me in a way that would’ve concerned guidance counselors across the nation.</i><br /><br /><b>Addicting!!</b><br /><br />I picked up the <b>Daimon</b> prequel in anticipation for the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9680718.Half_Blood__Covenant___1_" title="Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Half-Blood</a> ARC I’ll be reviewing soon and WOW! What a great kickoff to a series I know is going to have me on the edge of my seat. Definitely a storyline I can fall into with a great cast and a perfectly crafted paranormal element.<br /><br />The writing is exactly what I look for in a series, it’s edgy, sharp, and full of wit. The main character is crazy awesome. What’s not to love about Alexandria Andros?? She reminds me a ton of Rose from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/345627.Vampire_Academy__Vampire_Academy___1_" title="Vampire Academy (Vampire Academy, #1) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampire Academy</a> with her badassness that comes out full force when she lays the smack down on baddies. This girl knows how to fight and survive, and I can’t wait to jump into this series to experience her journey.<br /><br /><b>Daimon</b> is the prequel that sets the stage for the <i>Covenant</i> series and in this installment we meet Alex who is a half blood that was initially not worthy to train at the Covenant to serve the children of the gods. Alex and her pure blood mother fled the Covenant three years prior and have been in hiding and on the run since. That’s until a daimon attacked her mother and forced Alex to flee in search of the Sentinels and Guards she’s hoping will take her in.<br /><br />Definitely want the next book <i>NOW</i> as I can’t wait to see what happens next. Exciting!!<br /><br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br /><b>My notes about the book, not part of my review:</b><br />Hematoi or Ministers are pure blood spawn of demigods. They have startling eyes and can command one of the elements. They are protected by the Guards or Sentinels, but must not interact with each other.<br /><br />Guards or Sentinels are trained to fight at the Covenant in order to protect the purebloods from the daimons.<br /><br />Daimons thrived and fed on aether which is the essence of the gods and the very life force running through them. They are disguised by glamour and were once purebloods who have turned their back on the gods.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15394240210121805778" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Wendy Darling" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2745288-wendy-darling"><img alt="Wendy Darling" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379959930p2/2745288.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/166169753?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy Darling" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy Darling" href="/user/show/2745288-wendy-darling">Wendy Darling</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=heroines-butt-kicking">heroines-butt-kicking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=supportive">supportive</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=pn-demons">pn-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=2011-publication">2011-publication</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=read-2011">read-2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer166169753" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10430896763393638413"><b>Note: Info on free ebook download link for this story below.</b> A lot of authors release short stories as prequels or companion novels to their series, usually to keep fans jazzed between books or to entice you to try out the others. Some of these small bites are more successful than others, and I'm happy to report that the taste readers get from <i>Daimon</i> is enough to whet the appetite for more.<br/><br/>Alex is a 17-year-old half-demon who has been living among humans with her mother for three past years. She</span>
  <span id="freeText10430896763393638413" style="display:none"><b>Note: Info on free ebook download link for this story below.</b> A lot of authors release short stories as prequels or companion novels to their series, usually to keep fans jazzed between books or to entice you to try out the others. Some of these small bites are more successful than others, and I'm happy to report that the taste readers get from <i>Daimon</i> is enough to whet the appetite for more.<br /><br />Alex is a 17-year-old half-demon who has been living among humans with her mother for three past years. She doesn't know why they're hiding from The Covenant, but a brutal attack by relentless daimons forces her to go on run...possibly back to the very place her mother always told her they should avoid.<br /><br />This fast-paced, well-written short story does a great job of setting up the series. Alex is a smart, likable heroine with some mad daimon fighting skills. I really liked the action sequences in this book, as well as the way that the author shows the closeness between mother and daughter. (Ice cream always helps.) I got a little confused with one of the flashbacks, however, since it suddenly mentions a boy she's yearning for who hasn't been referenced before--I had to go back and skim through the book again to make sure I wasn't missing anything! But it's a small quibble considering how solid the rest of this preview is. It looks like this is going to be a really fun series and I'm looking forward to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9680718.Half_Blood__Covenant___1_" title="Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Half-Blood</a>, which comes out on September 15, 2011.<br /><br />Incidentally, contrary to what I assumed, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4476934.Jennifer_L__Armentrout" title="Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer L. Armentrout</a> is <i>not</i> the alter ego of urban fantasy author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/49024.Jennifer_Armintrout" title="Jennifer Armintrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer Armintrout</a>, who wrote the Blood Ties series. But readers who enjoy the other author's work will probably enjoy this YA series as well. <br /><br /><b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br />******************************************************<br /><br /><b>Download a Free Copy of Daimon</b><br /><br />This short story is currently listed at $3.99 pb/99 cents ebook on Amazon, but <a href="http://backinthemidnightgarden.blogspot.com/2011/05/daimon-review-free-download-link.html" rel="nofollow noopener">visit my blog for the link where you can download the free e-book</a>, which can be read on your e-reader or on your computer! Just scroll down to the bottom of the review. <br /><br /></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7487284018676882735"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/ja_zps16dd050b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Daimon is the prequel to the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. I have been planning to read this series for such a long time so I am finally taking the plunge and if this is any indication as to what to expect, I’m in for a wild ride.<br/><br/>Alexandria or Alex, is 17 years old. She is a half blood. Her mother was a Pure but her father was a mortal. She and her mother lived at the Covenant where she was trained for what role she would someday fulfill until suddenly, at age 14, her mother took h</span>
  <span id="freeText7487284018676882735" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/ja_zps16dd050b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410368345i/11098482.jpg" alt=" photo ja_zps16dd050b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Daimon is the prequel to the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. I have been planning to read this series for such a long time so I am finally taking the plunge and if this is any indication as to what to expect, I’m in for a wild ride.<br><br>Alexandria or Alex, is 17 years old. She is a half blood. Her mother was a Pure but her father was a mortal. She and her mother lived at the Covenant where she was trained for what role she would someday fulfill until suddenly, at age 14, her mother took her and fled. She never knew why, but for the last three years she and her mom had lived among the mortals in Miami, Florida. Alex never really did fit in even though she did try. Until one morning when her life was changed forever.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/girl_zpse5f474f0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410368345i/11098483.jpg" alt=" photo girl_zpse5f474f0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Daimons hunt Pures. They want the Aether from their blood. They usually aren’t all that interested in Half Bloods since their blood had such a smaller amount of Aether. Alex, who is 17 now, is on the run, on her own, trying to find her way to the nearest Covenant. But the Daimons are after her. She has no one. If she disappears, no one would even miss her. <br><br>This is a short story introducing us to Alex. I was blown away and can’t wait to delve deeper into this world. What Alex has already been forced to endure is breaking my heart. So, on I go to Half Blood. <br></span>

<div id="review_1549781889" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1549781889" />
    <a title="Tanya (Girl Plus Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/416997-tanya-girl-plus-books"><img alt="Tanya (Girl Plus Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1439375146p2/416997.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1549781889?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tanya (Girl Plus Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tanya (Girl Plus Books)" href="/user/show/416997-tanya-girl-plus-books">Tanya (Girl Plus Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780983157250" href="/book/show/11290005-daimon">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/416997-tanya-girl-plus-books?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/416997-tanya-girl-plus-books?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/416997-tanya-girl-plus-books?shelf=first-in-series">first-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/416997-tanya-girl-plus-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/416997-tanya-girl-plus-books?shelf=owned-physical-copy">owned-physical-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/416997-tanya-girl-plus-books?shelf=2016-shelf-love-challenge">2016-shelf-love-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1549781889" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15798102164761422801">Despite my deep and abiding love for all things Jennifer L. Armentrout, there was still one of her series that I had yet to start. I changed that over the weekend when I picked up the prequel to the Covenant series. This was a super short (60-something pages) introduction to the series but was still packed with plenty of action. It's interesting getting familiar with the world and the mythology of a new series. I've never read anything based on Greek mythology so the gods and demigods, etc are a</span>
  <span id="freeText15798102164761422801" style="display:none">Despite my deep and abiding love for all things Jennifer L. Armentrout, there was still one of her series that I had yet to start. I changed that over the weekend when I picked up the prequel to the Covenant series. This was a super short (60-something pages) introduction to the series but was still packed with plenty of action. It's interesting getting familiar with the world and the mythology of a new series. I've never read anything based on Greek mythology so the gods and demigods, etc are all new to me. I've seen some reviews that take issue with the series because apparently (at least the start of the series) is very similar to the Vampire Academy. Well, guess what... I haven't read the Vampire Academy series so any similarities will go right over my head. (Look at that, a little bonus to being behind on my TBR.) I enjoyed this one enough that I immediately picked up the next book, Half-Blood, and I'm excited to see where the series goes. Plus, I'm a sucker for JLA's male characters and I've heard plenty about Aiden and Seth. So let's be real - I'm way excited about meeting them. *cue the heart eyes* </span>
  <a data-text-id="15798102164761422801" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6256538868700679132">After reading book 1, I really don't think this prequel was necessary at all. I'll stick with my original 3 star rating because it didn't do anything <i>wrong</i>. It just didn't do much at all. This prequel covers what happens the hours leading up to book 1 and gives a super quick glimpse into the event(s) that kick start the series.   <span id="freeText6256538868700679132" style="display:none">After reading book 1, I really don't think this prequel was necessary at all. I'll stick with my original 3 star rating because it didn't do anything <i>wrong</i>. It just didn't do much at all. This prequel covers what happens the hours leading up to book 1 and gives a super quick glimpse into the event(s) that kick start the series. But this entire thing is recapped in about 2 pages in Half-Blood. And personally I would have been find skipping this. I was a perfect readathon audiobook and definitely piqued my interest for the series. But other than that, I don't think it actually added anything to the story.</span>

  <span id="freeText10390518105763355140" style="display:none">I've already enjoyed the author's Lux series and the first book I read from her Dark Elements series so I snatched this one up when I was in the mood for some good YA otherworld action.<br /><br />Daimon is a prequel that is more of a delicious teaser of what is to come for the Covenant series. It introduces the heroine, a few hints as to her background, an exciting chase, and then ends abruptly just in time for the reader to snack up the first book and settle in for an exciting ride.<br /><br />Alex sounds like a great heroine. She is definitely going to be her own hero and her own source of trouble all bundled into one. She has wry wit, a pragmatic outlook, and a core of strength. I liked her so far and look forward to continuing along with her story.</span>

<div id="review_231832773" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/231832773" />
    <a title="Kayleigh {K-Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3996633-kayleigh-k-books"><img alt="Kayleigh {K-Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540157695p2/3996633.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/231832773?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kayleigh {K-Books}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kayleigh {K-Books}" href="/user/show/3996633-kayleigh-k-books">Kayleigh {K-Books}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3996633-kayleigh-k-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer231832773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14161195152640930416"><a href='http://k-booksxo.blogspot.com/2011/11/daimon-covenant-05.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review of Daimon on K-Books</a><br/><br/>I really enjoyed this a lot more than I thought I would. Usually I don't enjoy prequels all that much as I feel like it's just an introduction into the 'real' story beginning. This one is definitely the exception. I really enjoyed Daimon. I thought it was a great start of a amazing story and I found myself getting completely hooked.<br/><br/>Alex is a Half-Blood. She is a descendent of the Gods, but her father was a mortal so that leaves her with two options, become a slave for </span>
  <span id="freeText14161195152640930416" style="display:none"><a href="http://k-booksxo.blogspot.com/2011/11/daimon-covenant-05.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Review of Daimon on K-Books</a><br /><br />I really enjoyed this a lot more than I thought I would. Usually I don't enjoy prequels all that much as I feel like it's just an introduction into the 'real' story beginning. This one is definitely the exception. I really enjoyed Daimon. I thought it was a great start of a amazing story and I found myself getting completely hooked.<br /><br />Alex is a Half-Blood. She is a descendent of the Gods, but her father was a mortal so that leaves her with two options, become a slave for the superior Pure-Bloods or become a Sentinel, a protector of the Pures, and fiht against the evil Pures-gone-bad Daimons. But that was before her mother pulls her out of training and goes on the run hiding from everyone from her old world, the Gods, the Pures and the Halfs without any explanation why. Alex doesn't feel like she belongs in this mortal world and then the unthinkable happens, the Daimons find her and Alex finds herself alone and fighting to get back to the school and the world in which she belongs.<br /><br />I think everyone planning to read this series should definitely read this before Half-Blood. I don't think my feelings while reading Half-Blood would have been quite the same if I hadn't read this before hand. It made the storyline that much more touching and at times heart-breaking.<br /><br />This prequel was incredible as far as prequels go and it's definitely the best prequel for a series I have ever read. It wasn't a boring introduction to the characters and the world as some prequels are. Yes it introduced you to the lead character but it was action-packed and fast-paced and I couldn't put it down. I read it in one sitting and it left me reeling and I had to pick Half-Blood up straight away.<br />An incredible start to an action-packed emotional series. I can't wait to see how things escalate from here.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14161195152640930416" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1324374416" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1324374416" />
    <a title="Elizabeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26365220-elizabeth"><img alt="Elizabeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460494912p2/26365220.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1324374416?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth" href="/user/show/26365220-elizabeth">Elizabeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780983157250" href="/book/show/11290005-daimon">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26365220-elizabeth?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26365220-elizabeth?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26365220-elizabeth?shelf=ya-romance">ya-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26365220-elizabeth?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26365220-elizabeth?shelf=donated">donated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26365220-elizabeth?shelf=hyped">hyped</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1324374416" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12964423531897948757"><b>Source:</b> I own a copy of this book.<br/><br/><b>Note:</b> These are my personal opinions. I received no outside person comments or opinions.<br/><br/>So during Christmas I got an Amazon gift card and bought 4 JLA books. Among them was this book, Half Blood, and the first two books of The Dark Elements Series. I am disappointed to say that I was not impressed with The Dark Elements Series but my viewpoint changed with this book.<br/><br/><b>Plot Summary:</b><br/><br/>Alex and her mother are on the run from the Convenient. (For unknown reasons. It was</span>
  <span id="freeText12964423531897948757" style="display:none"><b>Source:</b> I own a copy of this book.<br /><br /><b>Note:</b> These are my personal opinions. I received no outside person comments or opinions.<br /><br />So during Christmas I got an Amazon gift card and bought 4 JLA books. Among them was this book, Half Blood, and the first two books of The Dark Elements Series. I am disappointed to say that I was not impressed with The Dark Elements Series but my viewpoint changed with this book.<br /><br /><b>Plot Summary:</b><br /><br />Alex and her mother are on the run from the Convenient. (For unknown reasons. It wasn't explained.) They are surviving in the mortal world. Until Daimons track them down and kill Alex's mother and then try to kill her.<br /><br />Alex then decides to make the journey back to the very place her mother was hiding from. But her attempts are throttled when Daimons track her down.<br /><br /><b>My Reaction:</b><br /><br />I loved how the main character in this book was portrayed as a strong female heroine in some parts. She knows how to take care of herself and survive on her own.<br /><br />I was intrigued by all the action and drama in just these few short pages and that's always what draws me into a book series. Things need to happen for me to be engaged. <br /><br />I'm curious to see where JLA takes this series. Overall, I look forward to reading Half Blood.</span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6LNYpNgiJiBzb4iAP2Y8U49SnmHfSmQmFiajuSiGCiF2gkJhcgffmArH/XwhoWcAfGaZI6Xwl3/avJQEUDJ4PQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6XPxK1qhaWhqbQgYtcR5DyQbqQ0h/OwXDYO75Eg74nR3Quvu8ISQ0BPFfeSrAyJc1y+uT1tGH07BGYxZMI+QaA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText14329403433034608105" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
